          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkƒ±mƒ±zda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              We provide a seamlessly integrated all in one omni-channel marketing solution that enables organizations to engage in relationship marketing with their target audience, customers across complex marketing mix in an efficient and cost effective way.

Our clients can communicate with their target audience via e-mail, SMS, MMS, Social Media, Push Notifications, Whatsapp, Text to Speech (IVR) or any other channels they have...We provide a boutique solution through its easy integration feature and it makes campaign management much more efficient as a "centralized" solution.

When integrated into the organizations‚Äô CRM systems, SmartMessage tracks actions in many different fields such as customer interaction history, salesforce automation, lead management, marketing &amp; campaign management, service requests and complaints management, contact center automation, social media integration, customer loyalty and constantly provides feedback in these exact fields. In organizations using SmartMessage a "Customer Oriented" structure emerges.

Depending on our clients requirements, we can provide this service as an on-premise and/or on-cloud.
          </p>

          <dl class="mt-6">
              
    <div class="mb-2 flex papabear:mr-3 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:flex-wrap" data-test-id="about-us__website">
      <dt class="font-sans text-md font-bold text-color-text break-words w-40 papabear:flex-shrink-0 papabear:mr-3 mamabear:flex-shrink-0 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:mb-1">
          Web Sitesi

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Customers interact with brands across dozens of touchpoints ‚Äî websites, mobile apps, emails, push notifications, social media, and more.
But here‚Äôs the challenge:

Can you truly understand your customer without a single, unified view?

That‚Äôs where a Customer Data Platform (CDP) steps in, transforming fragmented data into rich, actionable insights.

üîç A CDP collects and unifies customer data from all channels
 üìä Builds real-time, comprehensive customer profiles
 ü§ñ Enables AI-powered predictions and personalized experiences

At SmartMessage, our advanced CDP takes it one step further:

- Likelihood scoring helps you identify who is most likely to convert
- Smart Timing ensures your message arrives at the perfect moment
- Next Best Channel guides you to the most effective engagement path

The result?

Smarter marketing. Greater ROI. Happier customers.

If you're looking to turn raw data into real connections, it‚Äôs time to explore SmartMessage CDP.
